\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{Sample__mod_8f90_source_l02254}02254 \textcolor{fortran_comment}{!    !> Return the covariance matrix of the input `Sample(nd,np)` of `np` points each of which has `nd` attributes (dimensions).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{Sample__mod_8f90_source_l02255}02255 \textcolor{fortran_comment}{!    !>}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{Sample__mod_8f90_source_l02258}02258 \textcolor{fortran_comment}{!    !> \(\backslash\)param[in]       Sample      :   The array of shape `(nd,np)` containing the sample.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{Sample__mod_8f90_source_l02259}02259 \textcolor{fortran_comment}{!    !> \(\backslash\)param[in]       Weight      :   The vector of length `np` of weights of the sample points (**optional**, default = `[(1\_IK, i = 1, np)]`).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{Sample__mod_8f90_source_l02260}02260 \textcolor{fortran_comment}{!    !> \(\backslash\)param[in]       Mean        :   The mean vector of the sample (**optional**, default = `[(0.\_RK, i = 1, nd)]`).}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{Sample__mod_8f90_source_l02273}02273 \textcolor{fortran_comment}{!        integer(IK)                         :: ip, sumWeight}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{Sample__mod_8f90_source_l02274}02274 \textcolor{fortran_comment}{!        Variance = 0.\_RK}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{Sample__mod_8f90_source_l02275}02275 \textcolor{fortran_comment}{!        if (present(Weight)) then}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{Sample__mod_8f90_source_l02276}02276 \textcolor{fortran_comment}{!            sumWeight = 0\_IK}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{Sample__mod_8f90_source_l02277}02277 \textcolor{fortran_comment}{!            do ip = 1,np}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{Sample__mod_8f90_source_l02278}02278 \textcolor{fortran_comment}{!                sumWeight = sumWeight + Weight(ip)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{Sample__mod_8f90_source_l02279}02279 \textcolor{fortran_comment}{!                Variance = Variance + Weight(ip) * ( Sample(1:nd,ip) -\/ Mean )**2}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{Sample__mod_8f90_source_l02280}02280 \textcolor{fortran_comment}{!            end do}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{Sample__mod_8f90_source_l02281}02281 \textcolor{fortran_comment}{!            Variance = Variance / real(sumWeight-\/1\_IK,kind=RK)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{Sample__mod_8f90_source_l02282}02282 \textcolor{fortran_comment}{!        else}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{Sample__mod_8f90_source_l02283}02283 \textcolor{fortran_comment}{!            do ip = 1,np}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{Sample__mod_8f90_source_l02284}02284 \textcolor{fortran_comment}{!                Variance = Variance + ( Sample(1:nd,ip) -\/ Mean )**2}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{Sample__mod_8f90_source_l02285}02285 \textcolor{fortran_comment}{!            end do}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{Sample__mod_8f90_source_l02286}02286 \textcolor{fortran_comment}{!            Variance = Variance / real(np-\/1\_IK,kind=RK)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{Sample__mod_8f90_source_l02287}02287 \textcolor{fortran_comment}{!        end if}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{Sample__mod_8f90_source_l02288}02288 \textcolor{fortran_comment}{!    end function getCovMatWeighted}}
